Page 17

Direct Trade of Chinese Silk

Miao Zhongxiu in Contact in New York

To Avoid Being Picked on by Foreign Merchants Again

Miao Zhongxiu, director of the Raw Silk Division of the Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, who was previously sent to the United States to inspect the silk industry, wrote from New York yesterday, stating that he had handled all three major tasks assigned to him on this trip to the United States. The first was to publicize the recent advantages of Chinese silk. Since arriving in the United States, he had visited hosiery and silk merchants in Chicago, New York, and various eastern provinces to publicize widely and to have the quality of the new silk samples recently sent from the Bureau checked by hosiery merchants and silk merchants. All said they were satisfied and said that Chinese silk could indeed compete with Japanese silk, that they would pay attention to using it in the future, and that they hoped that China would supply it in large quantities. This shows that the reputation of Chinese silk is gradually increasing in the United States. He hoped that Chinese silk merchants would improve and strive for progress. The second was to investigate the latest methods of inspecting raw silk in the United States. After arriving in New York, he visited the raw silk inspection center and saw that the raw silk inspection methods and machinery had been improved. He then practiced at the center for three weeks. For example, he was personally taught the inspection procedure for the nine-meter inspection of uniformity by weight calculation by the inventor. He would also adopt this method in his raw silk department after returning to China. The third, which he considered the most important and most difficult, was the issue of direct trade in Chinese silk. Because of changes in market prices, Chinese silk merchants were often picked on by foreign merchants when they paid for futures and suffered considerable losses. Direct trade was the only way to eliminate the drawbacks. After he came to the United States, he told American silk merchants about this matter. At the end of July, he hosted the leaders of American silk merchants at the New York International Office, with more than twenty people attending. At that time, he exchanged views with them on the proposal to form a direct trading company for Chinese silk (yellow, white, gray, warp) in Shanghai, New York, and Lyon. The attendees at the time said that if there was a proper way to gain the trust of the American market, they would very much approve. In recent days, he had been running around the New York silk merchants about this matter, and as soon as the contact was in order, he would pack up and return home and discuss the organization method with domestic silk industry groups and government agencies.

Workers at Various Silk Factories in Zhabei Went on Strike Again Yesterday

Opposing the Factory's Revision of the Wage System

Party and Government Agencies Send Personnel to Investigate the Truth

Da Gong She (L'Impartial) reported that workers at various silk factories in Shanghai went on strike in July of this year because their demands for wage restoration were not met. On July 8, it was resolved through mediation by the Social Affairs Bureau that wages would be increased by 5% (equivalent to 5 jiao). Recently, due to the decline in silk prices, the factories planned to revise the wages of female workers by implementing a production-based system, which was scheduled to be implemented on September 1. The Sixth Sericulture Workers' Union sent a letter to the Silk Industry Association requesting that the relevant measures be decided after being submitted to the Party and government for study. Unexpectedly, the Bao Tai and other factories on Chang'an Road announced that they would implement the production-based system across the board from September 1, which aroused resentment from the workers.

Joint Strike

More than 300 workers from the Bao Tai, Wu Xing, and other silk factories on Chang'an Road in Zhabei went on strike at 1:00 PM yesterday because they opposed the factory's adoption of a production-based system for wage distribution. At the same time, more than 2,000 workers from fourteen nearby factories, including Chu Xin, Fu Xing, Mao Feng, Fu Yuan, Yuan Xing and Yuan Ji on Yu Tong Road, Ji Yu on Gonghe Road, and Hong Tai on Guangfu Road, joined the strike after hearing about the Bao Tai strike, and the situation was quite serious.

Factories Not Stopped

As for the remaining silk factories, such as Feng Tai at Da Yang Bridge, Yu Tai at Tanzi Bay, Gong Da at Zhongxing Road, Fu Chang at Pengpu Bridge, Tian Sheng, Hong Yu, Ying Ji at Liuying Road, Yu Feng and Xing Lun at Gujiawan, Ding Feng, Mao Li, Xie Xin, Xie He, Hong Sheng, Yuan Xin, etc. at Yanjiage, the workers were satisfied with the method of reducing wages because they did not approve of changing the output system to pay wages. Therefore, they did not participate in the strike yesterday and continued to work as usual.

Union Persuasion

Since the workers of fourteen silk factories including Bao Tai went on joint strike, the Sixth District Sericulture Workers' Union was deeply afraid that the dispute would escalate. It immediately sent personnel to various factories to earnestly persuade the workers and instructed them to resume work as usual this morning. The issue of the wage system would be handled by the union to negotiate with various factories. However, whether it could resume normal work this morning could not be predicted.

Party and Government Investigate

After learning of the strike in the silk reeling factories in Zhabei, the Party and government agencies sent Fan Guoren, the cadre of the People's Movement Section of the Municipal Party Department, Zhao Rongchu, the cadre of the Third Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, and Fu Zhenbei, the director of the Second Precinct of the Fourth District, to the silk factories in Zhabei and the Sixth District Sericulture Workers' Union to investigate the truth in order to conduct mediation.

Labor Representatives Expressed

Da Gong She reporters met yesterday with people in charge of the Sixth District Sericulture Workers' Union, who said that the employers should be fully responsible for this labor unrest. On the 29th of last month, after the association received a notice from the Silk Factory Trade Association to change the wage system and implement the output system from September 1, it convened a meeting of all directors and supervisors to discuss the matter. It was resolved that the matter was of great importance. For the sake of improving the output of raw silk, the principle was very much in agreement. However, the detailed content of the system was not known to the union in advance. An inquiry was made to the trade association for more information, and in view of the urgency of the matter, it was requested to postpone implementation to avoid disputes. A letter was sent to the association for verification. On the one hand, opinions were prepared and submitted to the Party and government agencies on the 31st of last month, requesting supervision and leadership, and organizing a research committee. Labor and management, under the supervision of Party and government agencies, would jointly study a proper and average standard. After soliciting the consent of the worker representatives of various factories, labor and management would both benefit, and then the implementation issue could be discussed. The employer now suddenly implemented the destruction of the entire July 8 settlement decision, which caused the labor unrest, so the employer was really hard to blame. Now the association is doing its best to persuade the workers to resume work tomorrow and wait for the association to resolve the matter. Do not riot to cause a scandal.

Factory Should Report to Municipal Government If Industrial Bureau Interferes

City Chamber of Commerce Sends Letter to All Industries

Xin Sheng She (New Life News Agency) reported that the City Chamber of Commerce notified the Four National Goods Associations and various trade associations yesterday, saying: "Recently, the authorities of the Shanghai International Settlement have been interfering with various factories in the Settlement every month under the pretext of cracking down on dangerous businesses. The situation has been reported and transferred to the Municipal Government for serious negotiation. Now, the Shanghai Municipal Government Secretariat's letter No. 1250 states: 'The Government has repeatedly dispatched personnel to negotiate on the inspection of factories in the Settlement. It has been reported that the Industrial Bureau of the Settlement often interferes with factories in the Settlement under the pretext of cracking down on dangerous businesses. In the future, if the same event occurs, the factory should immediately report to the Government after receiving the notice from the Industrial Bureau so that personnel can be dispatched to investigate and verify the handling. It is hoped that your association will quickly transfer the order to the various factories and abide by it.' The association is hereby notified to comply."

The Results of Contacting the Association Were Still Good

It Was Decided to Make the Conference a Success

Shanghai-Beijing Through Train Yesterday

Once a Day, Takes Less Than Two Days Two Lines Implemented Simultaneously to Shorten Travel Time

North Station Opening Ceremony Extended to the 11th

The construction of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway North Station has been completed. The Traffic Department had originally planned to move in to work yesterday, but because the paint was not finished, it was decided to move in on the 5th and hold the opening ceremony on the 11th. At the same time, the public was invited to visit. The long-planned Shanghai-Beijing direct train began yesterday. The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou sections also shortened the travel time at the same time. The details of each item are as follows:

North Station Construction Completed, Postponed Move-In

After the new building of the North Station was completed on the 28th, except for the paint, the internal decoration, telephones, lights, water pipes, and painting were all completed. Therefore, the traffic department's original plan to move in today could not be done. According to Traffic Director Xie's remarks to the Xin Sheng She reporter, the report that the department had started moving in yesterday was unfounded. Now the department has postponed the official move-in to the 5th of this month.

Inauguration Ceremony

As for the inauguration of the North Station and the supplementary inauguration ceremonies for the two branch offices, originally scheduled to be held today in the new building, they have been postponed due to delays in construction. They are now officially scheduled for the 11th of this month. It is said that the Minister of Railways, Gu Mengyu, and the Vice Minister, Zeng Zhongming, will both attend the ceremony. At the same time, the Railway Bureau will invite people from all walks of life to visit the new site.

Through Train Service Between Shanghai and Peiping

The through train service between Shanghai and Peiping, jointly operated by the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway and the Peiping-Pukou Railway, has been in preparation for several months and has now been completed. It began operating yesterday morning, with one train running in each direction daily, taking 43 hours and 58 minutes. As the river ferry is not yet open, the Chengping Ferry will be used for connecting transportation. The two railway bureaus have also specially added one first-class and one second-class sleeping car, and the third and fourth-class cars are also the latest model steel cars. As for the fares, they will still be sold at the old prices.

The Labor Strike at British-American Tobacco Factory Turns Into a Labor-Management Dispute

The Stamp Department Resumes Work Yesterday Morning

The Crowd Angrily Surrounds and Prevents It

According to Da Gong She, since the internal dispute within the British-American Tobacco Company's New and Old Factories in Pudong, the situation has become increasingly severe. Hundreds of workers in the New Factory's Stamp Department petitioned the city government the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, they returned to the factory as usual, started the motors, and prepared to resume work. Upon hearing the news, workers in other departments became angry and immediately gathered more than 2,000 workers to surround the factory gate. The Public Security Bureau was informed and immediately dispatched a large number of police officers to the scene to suppress the situation. Fortunately, no incidents occurred. The Ministry of Finance's Taxation Department sent personnel yesterday to thoroughly investigate and mediate. The details are recorded separately below.

Resumption of Work

The Second Factory of British-American Tobacco Company in Lujiazui has more than 5,000 male and female workers. Since participating in the general strike, internal opinions have suddenly diverged. More than 600 workers in the Stamp Department questioned the union and advocated resuming work. The day before yesterday, they sent more than 100 representatives to petition the city government, requesting that the Public Security Bureau be instructed to send police to protect the workers. Yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, these workers entered the factory and immediately started the motors to prepare for work, which aroused the anger of workers in other departments.

Surrounding the New Factory

After the workers in the Stamp Department and other departments of the New Factory entered the factory and started the motors, workers in other departments believed that they were intentionally disrupting the strike order. They immediately joined forces with more than 2,000 workers from the Old Factory and went to surround the New Factory from all sides. More than 300 workers rushed into the factory building, intending to forcibly stop the work. The situation suddenly became serious.

Dispatching Police to Suppress

The Municipal Public Security Bureau, according to the report from Cai Yuantang, captain of the Second Brigade of the stationed petitioning police, instructed more than 30 long-term police officers to cooperate with all the police officers of the Second Detachment of the Security Team, as well as hundreds of petitioning police officers in the factory. Fully armed, they were deployed around the perimeter. Inspector Li and others, together with all the directors and supervisors of the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union, contacted Li Dehe, a Western staff member of the factory, to temporarily suspend work until the labor unrest was resolved, so as to prevent the dispute from escalating. As a result, the factory expressed its acceptance and immediately shut down all the motors. At the same time, the police officers persuaded the workers surrounding the outside of the factory separately. They dispersed at about 11:00 AM.

Party Headquarters Summoning

Since the Municipal Party Headquarters received a petition from the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union requesting a thorough investigation, it was deeply concerned that the labor unrest would become more severe and difficult to manage. In order to clarify the internal opinions of the workers, the Civil Affairs Section summoned Pan Quanrong, Zhang Xiqi, Chen Shengkui, Xu Wenqing, and Chen Siming, workers in the Stamp Department of the New Factory, to the department for questioning and gave them strict advice, ordering them to wait quietly for the Party and government to mediate according to law before the labor unrest was resolved, so as to avoid causing unexpected disputes.

Song Will Mediate

The Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union believed that the labor unrest had been mediated by the Party and government several times, but no solution had been reached. Therefore, it sent a letter to Finance Minister Song requesting him to act as a mediator. After receiving the report, Song believed that the labor unrest had been delayed without resolution and would affect the national tax revenue. Yesterday, he specially sent Zhang, a staff member of the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance, to Pudong to investigate the truth from the factory and the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union, so as to conduct mediation at an opportune time.

Municipal Government Decides

The Municipal Government, considering that the labor and management of the British-American Tobacco Company have been deadlocked for a long time and have not yet been resolved, has specially formulated a solution and ordered the Social Affairs Bureau to order both labor and management to abide by it. The content is as follows: 1. The dismissal of worker Fang Fuqi is approved. 2. Worker No. 146 should be reinstated. 3. Wages should be paid as usual during the strike period of all workers in the Old Factory, and 70% of the wages should be paid for the affected parts. Wages should be paid at half price during the strike period of all workers in the New Factory. After receiving the order, the Social Affairs Bureau instructed both parties to comply yesterday.

Request to Stop

The Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union reported to the Party and government agencies: This is an urgent report. We have learned that Pan Quanrong and other workers in the New Stamp Department have been used by the factory to incite workers to resume work, arousing public outrage among workers in the New and Old Factories. We have already reported this. Unexpectedly, this morning at 7:00 AM, Pan Quanrong and others entered the factory and still started the motors first. The whole factory was in turmoil. There were thousands of people gathered in front of the department, unanimously demanding that the department immediately stop working. The Westerners in the department, fearing that conflicts would occur and damage the machines, ordered the motors to stop. After hearing the news, our union immediately entered the factory with all the directors and supervisors to maintain order and prevent accidents. It has been found that there are hundreds of workers in the department, and only a few of them are willing to work. They are being forced to resume work by Pan Quanrong, who is using the power of the factory, and it is not voluntary. The total number of workers in the factory is more than 8,000. How can a small number of bad elements be allowed to undermine unity? Although the department has stopped working, Pan and others are still thinking about starting the motors. If they continue to incite public outrage and damage the factory's machines, our union will be unable to bear the responsibility. Therefore, we urgently report and request an immediate stop. Respectfully submitted to the Municipal Party Headquarters.

General Union Investigation

The Shanghai General Labor Union believes that the general strike of the workers of the British-American Tobacco Factory is a struggle against international capitalism and is of great significance to the entire labor movement. Now that it has learned that internal opinions have arisen in the factory, causing labor-management disputes, it believes that this is unfavorable to the future. Therefore, it has specially sent personnel to investigate the truth, so as to persuade both parties not to be used by private individuals and to unite and struggle to achieve the final victory.

Fourth District Declaration

Yesterday, the Fourth District Cigarette Industry Union issued a declaration of assistance for the British-American labor unrest: International capitalists rely on their unequal treaties as a talisman to open up markets in China and implement their economic aggression. They use their terrifying means to oppress our hard-working and weak workers. This time, the workers of the British-American Tobacco Factory, unable to withstand the factory's repeated destruction, resolutely responded with a general strike. In addition to upholding the friendship of the same class, our union vows to be a strong supporter. We hope that all workers will align their steps and make a strong struggle. This is our declaration.

Zhang Danru and Others Petition to Organize a Gold and Silver Exchange

According to Xin Xin She, the merger of the city's Gold Exchange and the Gold Department of the Securities and Commodities Exchange has not been resolved due to differing opinions between the two parties. Now, gold merchants Zhang Danru, Yu Huancheng, Sheng Chunlin, etc., have initiated the establishment of the Shanghai Gold and Silver Exchange. They have submitted a document to the Social Affairs Bureau to be forwarded to the Municipal Government for consultation with the Ministry of Industry. The Social Affairs Bureau's document to the Municipal Government is copied below: According to the petition submitted by merchants Zhang Danru and others, We, Danru and others, have been engaged in commerce in Shanghai and have been trading in margin gold on the Shanghai Securities and Commodities Exchange and the Gold Exchange. Looking at the world situation, although there are many countries that use gold, silver is indispensable. Our country is a silver-using country, and Shanghai is a gathering place for foreign trade. The price difference between gold and silver is considerable. It relies entirely on the fair market price set by the exchange to stabilize it. Recently, we have heard that the business term of the Shanghai Securities and Commodities Exchange and the Gold Exchange has expired and they cannot be merged according to law. Although they are still actively negotiating, the two parties have differing opinions. In the extreme case, it is difficult to get close. We are afraid that the government, in order to maintain the authority of the law, may not listen to their protracted delay and order them to disband. If the transaction is suspended, all foreign trade merchants will be greatly affected. Therefore, we have gathered twenty like-minded colleagues to initiate the organization of a Shanghai Gold and Silver Exchange Co., Ltd. The total capital is 1 million yuan, divided into 50,000 shares, each share worth 20 yuan. All the shares have been fully subscribed by the founders. Once the government approves, we can collect the share capital and establish it on a fixed date in accordance with legal procedures. The exchange will not have to worry about suspension, and foreign trade merchants will be spared the pain of gold price hikes. It is reasonable to check the provisions of Article 1 of the Implementing Rules of the Exchange Law, and separately submit a petition stating the facts and submit it to your bureau for review and approval. Enclosed are three copies of the original petition. Accordingly, in addition to submitting it to the Ministry of Industry for review and approval in accordance with the law and issuing instructions, we have enclosed the original petition and respectfully submit it to your Excellency for review and approval, and forward it to the Ministry of Industry for review and approval. Respectfully submitted.

Kidnapping Attempt Fails, Gunmen Fire Two Shots at Victim

Textile Magnate Xu Luqing Encountered Danger Yesterday Morning

Shot and Wounded, Life Not in Imminent Danger

Vehicle Number 16669 Suspect

At around 9:30 yesterday morning, a case of failed kidnapping and shooting of the victim occurred on Haig Road, Jing'an Temple. The details are described below.

Gang's Covetousness

Xu Luqing, a Ningbo native, is 47 years old and lives at No. 167 Yuyuan Road. He has two sons, the eldest son, Ruifu, is 26 years old, and the youngest son, Kuifu, is 21 years old. Both work in the Kenye and Heli Banks. Xu himself is a broker at No. 42 on the Cotton Exchange and runs the Yiyuan Cotton Yarn Company. Because Xu is by nature stingy and thrifty in managing his family, he has accumulated some wealth over the years. This has aroused the covetousness of the gang. However, Xu has long been wary, so he changes his attire frequently when he goes out every day, or even avoids certain roads.

Sudden Kidnapping

Unexpectedly, at around 9:30 yesterday morning, Xu left his home on foot. When he arrived at the public bus stop in front of the Happy Barber Shop at No. 27 Haig Road, Jing'an Temple Road, three kidnappers suddenly appeared by the roadside. One was wearing a Western suit and shirt, one was wearing a white silk long gown, and one was wearing short clothes. The kidnapper in the white long gown stepped forward and grabbed Xu's left hand, dragging him violently. At that time, Xu was panicked and struggled desperately to escape, intending to flee into the Happy Barber Shop. Seeing this, the kidnapper in the Western suit stepped forward and grabbed Xu. Seeing that the situation was critical, Xu fell to the ground.

Two Shots Fired

When he shouted "Kidnapping!", two Russian public bus ticket inspectors, No. 44 and No. 62, happened to be waiting for a bus at the public bus stop at that location. Hearing the urgent shouts, they ran to the scene to check and tried to rescue Xu. Unexpectedly, they were threatened back by the kidnapper in the Western suit with a gun. At the same time, the kidnapper in the white long gown drew his gun and fired two shots at Xu. The kidnapper in the Western suit also tried to turn around and fire, but the bullets jammed and he did not fire. The kidnappers panicked and immediately jumped into a black-licensed vehicle with the Concession registration number 16669, which was parked by the roadside in advance, and sped away south on Haig Road.

Life Can Be Saved

At that time, Indian Constable No. 671 at the traffic post at the intersection of Haig Road had received a police report and saw the vehicle speeding away. Unable to catch up, he quickly drew his gun and fired five shots at the kidnappers' vehicle. It is not yet known whether he hit the vehicle. He immediately returned to send Xu to the Haig Road Red Cross Hospital for treatment and reported to the police station, which dispatched detectives to pursue the kidnappers in all directions. After Xu Luqing was sent to the hospital, the hospital examined him and found that he had been shot twice, once in the leg and once in the lower abdomen. Fortunately, the intestines and bladder were not damaged, so his life was not in great danger. The bullets remained in the abdomen and will be removed by surgery. As of 12:00 last night, the kidnappers' vehicle had not been found. At the same time, it is still questionable whether the vehicle's registration number is 16669. All police stations have notified all police agencies in the city to assist in the pursuit.

Robbers Open Fire By Mistake, Killing Accomplice

One Robber Arrested, Confesses Details

On July 5 of this year, at 10:30 AM, Chen Longhe, the accountant of Yisheng Rubber Factory at No. 83 Binlang Road, and Cai Alai, the owner of Dafeng Tobacco Paper Store at No. 904 Xiaoshadu Road, were returning after withdrawing money from the Salt Industry Bank on Robert Sheng Road. When they passed near Binlang Road, Xiaoshadu Road, they were suddenly encountered by four robbers. One of them held a handgun and blocked their way, hoping to rob them. Chen and others shouted for help and desperately fled. Seeing that the situation was not good, the robber with the gun immediately fired a shot. Unexpectedly, the bullet hit his accomplice, Yin Laowu, in a vital spot. He was injured and fell inside Da Xu Li Lane. Chen and others were able to take the opportunity to escape without loss. When the patrolmen arrived after hearing the alarm, the gang had already fled without a trace. The injured robber Yin Laowu was taken to the hospital, but he died en route due to his serious injuries. He was then sent to the coroner's office for examination. At around 7:00 AM the day before yesterday, Chinese Detective Hua Men and Chinese Detective Wang Yongjun of the Jing'an Temple Police Station arrested one of the robbers, Hong Shengzhang (aka Wang Dadaizi), an Anhui native, on Ningbo Road and took him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, the police lawyer, presented the case and requested that the defendant be detained for investigation. When questioned, the defendant Hong Shengzhang confessed that he, the fugitive Hua Deming, Liu Haiqing, and the deceased had discussed the matter in advance at Hua's home. Hua held the gun, and I was on lookout behind. At the time, the victim shouted, so Hua fired the gun, but mistakenly killed his accomplice Yin Laowu. Judge Xue Lanru verified the confession and ordered Hong to be detained for seven days for investigation.

Aftermath of a Brothel Rivalry

Yang Keming's Love Affair Creates Trouble

Lu Qingyang Involved, Suspended from Duty

Feng Xiuzhen, also known as Yifei Laoqi, a prostitute at the Fuyu Li No. 6 brothel on Yunnan Road, although past her prime, still retains her charm and has the ability to captivate the public. Last year, she entered into a blood oath alliance with Yang Keming, a handsome young man from Ningbo. This year, she formed an inextricable bond with Shi Jinnan, a wealthy merchant from Yue. Unexpectedly, the old and new lovers gathered unexpectedly the other night, and the jealous rivalry created waves. Yang held a pre-agreement ticket stating that the prostitute agreed to marry him, accused Shi of adultery with his fiancée, and filed a complaint with the police station. After investigation, the police found that the note was written unilaterally by Yang and was nothing more than a blackmail attempt against Shi. Yang and Han Shuiqiao, who helped him defraud, were taken into custody by the First Special District Court the next morning. The details were detailed in yesterday's newspaper. We have learned that Laoqi strongly denied that she had agreed to the note submitted by Yang. However, their love had reached a considerable level at normal times, and during their intimate moments, Laoqi had expressed her intention to devote herself to Yang. However, she requested that Yang pay off her 1,500 yuan debt, but Yang was unable to raise the large sum of money, so she remained a public woman. That evening, when he saw Shi Jinnan pluck the flower, and there were many guests present, he felt even more embarrassed and hurriedly left. He gathered four or five friends and went to catch the adulterer the next morning, resulting in legal trouble. Afterwards, the police station considered that there was more than just Han Shuiqiao accompanying Yang, so they waited for the court to question and interrogated Yang about his accomplices. He confessed that Lu Qingyang, a fellow villager living at No. 621 Tiantong Road, had also participated in the day's events. Lu is currently working as a clerk in a certain agency. The police head then dispatched Feng Xiushan, the detective in charge of the case, to arrest Lu. The day before, at the end of August, Lu received his monthly salary. His superiors dismissed him from his position because he had committed a criminal offense. Yesterday morning, Detective Feng escorted Lu to the First Special Court, where Judge Feng Shide presided over the interrogation. Police Lawyer Ru Baoyi stated the case and requested that Lu be held in custody to wait for the interrogation with Yang Keming, Han Shuiqiao, etc. on September 7. Lu also hired Lawyer Ye Shaoying to defend him in court. The court approved the police's request and ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and rescheduled for interrogation on September 7.

Ministry of Communications Prepares Sino-British Communications

Trainees Returning to Shanghai from England

The Ministry of Communications' International Telecommunications Bureau is preparing for Sino-British communications. Since a large number of machines have been shipped to Shanghai one after another, the bureau has transported them to the newly built radio station in Zhenru for assembly. It is reported that 70% of the machines have been shipped to Shanghai for assembly. The remaining machines will arrive in Shanghai completely in mid-month. As for the trainees sent by the Ministry of Communications to England to practice communications, they will arrive in Shanghai at the end of this month. After the trainees arrive in Shanghai, they will be sent to the radio station to test Sino-British communications. The communication date was originally set for October 1, but it has been decided to postpone it for one month due to concerns that the assembly of machines and other matters may not be completed as scheduled.

Jointly Forming a Social Science Research Association

The study of social sciences has gradually attracted the attention of public and private institutions in China this year, and there has been considerable development. However, the division of labor and cooperation is not fully implemented due to the lack of liaison mechanisms. In view of this, the Chinese Economic Society and the Chinese Statistical Society have initiated the establishment of the Chinese Social Science Research Committee to promote the research of social sciences throughout the country and its division of labor and cooperation. In addition to the above two societies, the participating groups include the Academia Sinica, the Peiping Social Survey Institute, the Nankai University School of Economics, the Investigation Section of the National Tariff Commission, the Chinese Economic and Statistical Research Institute, the Jiaotong University Research Institute, the China Branch of the Pacific International Institute, the Research Department of the Sun Yat-sen Culture and Education Museum, the Lingnan University School of Economics and Politics, and the Logistics School's Economics and Politics Special Class, etc., more than ten institutions. The committee members are Ma Yinchu, Liu Dajun, Zhang Jia'ao, Jia Shiyi, Wu Chaochang, He Dekui, Dai Kexie, Li Zhaohuan, Li Quanshi, Wang Zhongwu, Wu Dajian, Zhu Junyi, Zhang Xinyi, Sheng Jun, Lin Wei, Sun Zheng, Tao Menghe, He Lian, Cai Zimin, Zhong Rongguang, Yang Duanliu, Hu Shi, Xu Xinliu, Zhou Zuomin, and other twenty-four people. Liu Dajun was elected as Chairman, He Lian as Vice Chairman, Sheng Jun as Secretary, and Xu Xinliu as Accountant. Zhou Yabo was also hired as an executive. Letters were sent to various research institutions to investigate their completed, ongoing, and planned work, and to solicit suggestions from various institutions on the division of labor and cooperation. As for rural economic research, because many institutions are conducting research, the standing committee members have directly investigated the progress of the research and reported the results to all committee members.

Chinese Youth Explorer Returns Successfully After Overcoming Difficulties

Only One Person Left in the Sixteen-Member Team, All Separated Midway

Spent More Than a Year Traveling Through Dozens of Provinces, Experiencing All Kinds of Difficulties

Chen Yiqin, a Chinese youth world explorer, embarked on a long-distance exploration from Guangzhou in June last year. He passed through Shanghai and went north in April of this year. After more than a year, and having endured all kinds of hardships, he has completed his work and set off south in [the previous] month, arriving in Shanghai yesterday (September 1). After resting for a day or two, he will take a boat to Guangdong to return home. According to Chen Yiqin's account to reporters, the details of his trip are as follows:

Motivation for Departure

According to Chen, I have seen that the Chinese people do not pay attention to the customs and practices of various parts of the country, and have no adequate understanding of the world situation. In this state, we cannot consolidate our own position, nor can we compete with other countries in technology. The result will inevitably be failure. In order to strengthen the race, save the country, and improve the international position, I initiated the organization of the Youth World Exploration Team with my siblings and relatives. The initial members of the team included Lin Xiehe and others, a total of sixteen people. The purpose of our team's exploration is: 1. To seek out hidden and secret places to uncover the riddles of hundreds of years ago; 2. To investigate local customs and practices and compile them into magazines for the world; 3. To take unique activity films on the ground and contribute the results to the people of the world.

Exploratory Experiences

When our team set off for Fuzhou, my younger brother, Yike, fell into the river while crossing a bridge and was seriously injured. Therefore, I returned to Guangdong to treat my brother, but the medicine proved ineffective, and he eventually passed away. My colleagues and I revived our ambitious endeavor in December, traveling from Guangdong to Shanghai, then to Beijing and Hebei, covering more than ten provinces. This journey lasted for over a year. Due to various setbacks, some comrades feared to proceed and separated midway, leaving only one person remaining to this day. The perilous experiences encountered can be summarized in five points: ㈠ the death of my brother, Yike; ㈡ encountering bandits in Huizhou, where one comrade was killed, and although all our belongings were looted, I managed to escape; ㈢ encountering a severe storm at sea, which caused our ship to sink. I floated on a lifebuoy for three days and nights, without food or drink, until I was rescued in Shantou; ㈣ being attacked in Shanghai, where a villain demanded my national passport but failed, almost succeeding in harming me; ㈤ participating in the front lines of the war against Japan until the Sino-Japanese peace agreement was signed, after which I left the military. The above are all the perilous experiences I encountered but managed to survive.

Future Plans

During this trip, I obtained many major local products and antiques. Whenever I arrived at a location, I would record the circumstances in writing and send them to Guangdong in installments, intending to compile them into a book for the reference of our countrymen. The team's work plan is divided into five phases, the details of which have been published in newspapers in the provinces we have traveled through. Since the anti-Japanese war in the Northeast, the second phase of our work has come to an end. I plan to return to the province to compile a report and then undertake the third phase of our exploration work. The itinerary for the third phase is planned to depart from Hong Kong, passing through Guangdong, Guangxi, Yunnan, the South Seas Islands, India, Nepal, Bhutan, Tibet, Xikang, Sichuan, Guizhou, Hunan, and ending in Jiangxi, with an estimated duration of two years. After completing the tour of China, I will then travel to Europe to explore various countries around the world.

Compatriots Invent Water-Powered Motor

After the successful invention of the water-powered motor (i.e., self-powered engine) by Zhejiang residents Shan Chunqiao and Chen Xinbiao, news of the event has been repeatedly reported in the newspapers. It is now known that prominent figures in Shanghai's industrial circles, after reading the reports, have flocked to see it. The road to the workshop is filled with visitors. However, the inventors, as the motor is currently being submitted to the central government for patent protection, are unable to display it for public viewing at this time. They deeply apologize to those who have traveled to visit but have been politely declined. The research process involved ten years of painstaking effort, with over a hundred failures, ultimately leading to bankruptcy before achieving success. Their spirit of perseverance and resilience is truly commendable and marks a new record in China's scientific community. Therefore, they are temporarily keeping their life's work a secret until it is ready for public demonstration. It is reported that many people in the industrial sector are contacting the inventors. To facilitate communication, a preparatory office has been set up at No. 22, Jiujiang Road, 3rd Floor, in the Shanghai International Settlement, and a temporary factory has also been established to produce prototypes for testing. It is scheduled to invite the press to visit sometime in the middle of the month.

Municipal Health Bureau Opens Municipal South Clinic

The Municipal Health Bureau, recognizing the dense population and numerous diseases in the Nanshi area, has established that although there are a few public and private medical facilities, most of them charge high fees, making them inaccessible to those who are not wealthy. Furthermore, since the January 28th Incident, all industries in the city have been in decline, the economy has deteriorated, and unemployment has increased. Therefore, the need for free medical care is more pressing than ever. A request was submitted to the Municipal Government for an appropriation of 4,800 yuan for establishment costs and 1,000 yuan per month for recurring expenses. Seven municipal houses in Yude Lane, Penglai Road, in the central area of Nanshi, were rented and converted into a clinic. Currently, workers have been hired to renovate the buildings and install all necessary equipment inside. The clinic is expected to be completed and open for consultations in the middle of this month. The clinic will have departments of internal medicine, surgery, otolaryngology, obstetrics, venereology, pediatrics, and physical therapy, all staffed by experienced physicians.

Page 19

Wenzhou Shipping Competition

Haiyan Ship Suspends Service

Xinfeng Ship to be Transferred

Since the China Merchants Bureau discussed opening the Ruiping ferry service in Wenzhou, it has sparked competition among various smaller shipping companies, leading to a maritime battle. Both sides have been exerting all their efforts to attack each other, resulting in the unfortunate suspension of the Haiyan ship, with all its crew members laid off, adding to the number of unemployed. The struggle is still ongoing.

Small Ships Unite The China Merchants Bureau has always had a dominant and profitable position in Wenzhou shipping. Recently, various small ships from Nanshi added Wenzhou services, also operating at smaller inland piers. As a result, a large number of passengers and cargo have been taken away by these smaller ships. Therefore, the old plan was revived this year to implement the Ruian-Pingyang route proposed by Guo Wai-feng to make up for the lack of cargo transportation. Bureau members, such as Wang Heqing, were specially dispatched to Ruiping for inspection, preparing for the opening of the service. This caused unease among the various Wenzhou ferry services in Nanshi. Since Ruiping is a small inland pier, if the China Merchants Bureau were to operate ships there, the smaller shipping companies on the same route would be difficult to compete with and would inevitably fail. Therefore, the smaller shipping companies have also taken immediate action. First, the Ruiping ferry services were united, and then personnel were sent to Ruiping to sign annual packaging contracts with various passengers at low rates, preventing the China Merchants Bureau from gaining a foothold.

China Merchants Bureau Strives The China Merchants Bureau is determined not to give up due to its business interests. Therefore, on the one hand, the Guangji ship was sent to the factory for major repairs, preparing to operate the Ruiping service. On the other hand, it approached Yili Company in Nanshi, intending to lease its new Yili ships at favorable prices to reduce business obstacles. However, this was rejected by Yili and others. The China Merchants Bureau had to find other ships to operate. The Haiyan ship, which originally operated on the route, was superior to other smaller ships in terms of speed and passenger capacity. Therefore, it first competed in passenger transportation. The Haiyan ship only took 28 hours to travel from Wenzhou to Shanghai, while smaller ships in Nanshi took two days and nights. Therefore, most passengers preferred to take the Haiyan, which impacted the business of the smaller ships. As a result, the second struggle ensued.

Ministry of Transportation Orders The Ministry of Transportation recently issued an order to the China Merchants Bureau, stating that according to a petition from various public organizations and people in Yongjia County, the China Merchants Bureau's Haiyan ship is over 60 years old. According to maritime regulations, ships older than 30 years are not allowed to operate. The China Merchants Bureau is using an old and decaying ship to operate between Shanghai and Wenzhou, carrying passengers and treating the lives of the people of Wenzhou as child's play. It should be strictly ordered to suspend service to ensure maritime safety. Upon receiving this order, Liu Hongsheng immediately ordered the shipping department to suspend the Haiyan ship's service, and all its staff were dismissed. In addition to the business staff who were laid off, the navigation and engine personnel, as well as all the sailors, were temporarily retained by the bureau, waiting for vacancies to arise and being given priority for reemployment. However, there are no current positions available, further increasing the number of unemployed. The Xinfeng Ship Changes Course The Haiyan ship's suspension was caused by secret attacks from others. The China Merchants Bureau is therefore more actively competing for the Wenzhou route, determined not to let it be monopolized by a few and easily give up. The Jiahe ship has been temporarily dispatched as a substitute, and the Xinfeng ship from the Northern Ocean route is planned to be transferred to the Wenzhou route. Its speed is faster than the Haiyan, and its passenger capacity is even better. A third wave of competition is bound to occur after this ship starts operating.

Claims White Russians are Deliberately Spreading Rumors

Decides to Host Press Today

We remitted 120,007 yuan to the general, with the first remittance of 3,000 yuan, the second remittance of 10,000 yuan, the third remittance of 25,000 yuan, and the fourth remittance of 13,500 yuan through the Bank of Communications, totaling 51,500 yuan. Our company initiated the collection of these donations to support the anti-Japanese military and encourage the anti-Japanese generals. National Silk Exhibition Closes Yesterday

Representative of the Ministry of Industry Presents Five Suggestions

Hoping the Silk Industry Will Make Improvements

The Chinese National Silk Exhibition, co-organized by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Silk Industry Bank, the Silk Industry Association, and the Electrical Silk Weaving Factory Association, has been on display since July 10th on the third and fourth floors of the Tianhou Palace Bridge, lasting over fifty days. The exhibition was scheduled to close yesterday afternoon at 2 PM in the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce issued notice to all parties to participate and asked party and government agencies to send people to give speeches. Representatives from hundreds of businesses attended. The Ministry of Industry and the Municipal Government also sent representatives to give instructions. The event is summarized as follows:

Order of Ceremony

㈠ Ringing the bell to open the meeting, ㈡ Paying the highest respect to the Party, the national flag, and the portrait of the Premier, ㈢ Chairman respectfully reciting the Premier's will, ㈣ Chairman's speech, ㈤ Vice-Chairman's report on the progress of the exhibition, ㈥ Speech by the representative of the Ministry of Industry, ㈦ Speech by the Mayor, ㈧ Speeches, ㈨ Guided tour, ㈩ Closing.

Chairman's Speech

First, Chairman Wang Xiaolai gave a speech, saying, "Today is the closing day of the Chinese National Silk Exhibition. We remember that at the opening last month, the three-day art and recreation event caused a sensation, and tens of thousands of people flocked here. At that time, the weather was extremely hot, but everyone was not afraid of the heat and came to participate. Today, the weather has turned cooler, but the number of guests is not as many as at the opening, which shows that everything in the world depends on people's efforts. The more lively the efforts, the more people will participate. This exhibition was originally sponsored by manufacturers and people from all walks of life, and we have achieved such good results. Because the scheduled period has expired, we are closing today. However, although the closing is only a formality, we will continue to work hard. I hope that everyone's enthusiasm will not also close from now on. Chinese silk relies on rural sericulture. Now, China's rural areas have no way out, and the sericulture industry is particularly declining. The crisis is getting deeper day by day. All those engaged in industry must first find a way out for Chinese silk and a market for cocoons. If we seek this, then our sense of responsibility will never close."

President's Report

Next, the association's Vice-President Wang Yansong reported, "Today, China's industry and commerce are declining, and goods cannot be sold smoothly due to the influx of foreign goods. The decline of the silk industry is a fatal blow to China's industry and commerce. The four organizations of this association have prepared the silk exhibition in order to promote domestic silk. The Shanghai Mayor was invited to be the honorary president, and the preparation period was about one month. The exhibition lasted for a total of fifty-two days. Hundreds of manufacturers participated with more than 430 kinds of goods. Special issues were published in five newspapers, including the News Daily, Morning Post, Current Affairs News, China Daily, and Shanghai Business News, to promote the exhibition. The total cost was over 6,000 yuan. At present, more than 4,000 yuan have been moved from the Silk Industry Bank and the Municipal Government, and more than 2,000 yuan are still waiting for assistance from the Social Affairs Bureau and other places. It is estimated that the average number of visitors during the exhibition was more than 5,000 people per day, totaling 300,000 people. These more than 300,000 people have a deep impression of domestic silk. It was originally intended to award various prizes to the manufacturers today, but all the awards from the Ministry of Industry have not yet been issued. They will be sent back after Minister Chen returns to Beijing and then forwarded by each association to the manufacturing plants."

Instructions from the Ministry of Industry

Next, Ji Zejin, the special representative of the Ministry of Industry, delivered a speech, saying, "All of you present here are enthusiastic supporters of promoting domestic products. However, we should study why domestic silk cannot be sold well abroad. From my observation, there are several reasons: ㈠ Domestic silk has no uniform standard, such as length and scale are often inconsistent, and the quality of materials also changes, so it is difficult to gain the trust of foreigners. ㈡ Domestic silk is mostly plain and has few prints and bright colors, which is not popular with foreign women and children, so improvements should be made in terms of patterns and colors. ㈢ Domestic silk is too heavy and thick, while foreigners prefer thin and soft materials. ㈣ Chinese people often act alone in foreign trade, with little cooperation and no advertising power to occupy the market. After this, the remedies should be to print the quality, value, color, and style of each product into a booklet so that salesmen can take them to various countries for promotion. ㈤ More domestic products are sold indirectly and fewer are sold directly. They cannot be sold directly from other people's hands. I hope that in the future, we will unite and work together to seek overseas markets."

Mayor's Instructions

Next, the Mayor's representative, Pan Gongzhan, gave instructions, saying, "There are two points of this meeting that are deeply worthy of our memory. I hope that everyone will preserve this spirit: ㈠ The products exhibited this time are different from the past. There has been progress in all aspects, whether it is color or material. There are many products that one cannot believe are domestic goods. The effect of the exhibition is to make the public know that domestic goods can also be compared with foreign goods. ㈡ The Silk Industry Bank and other groups have jointly managed this meeting, which is gratifying. From the producers to the sellers, they have worked together. This spirit is unprecedented in other banks. This can be said to be the pioneer. I hope that in the future, not only the banking industry can be like this, but all sectors should uphold this spirit of cooperation to revitalize everything. Then this meeting is not only an exhibition in nature, but can also be a model for the general public."

Silk Industry Thanks

Next, Lu Zhengbing, the chairman of the Shanghai Silk Industry Association, gave a speech, saying, "Today is the closing ceremony of the Chinese National Silk Exhibition. We are honored to have representatives from the Party, government, industry, commerce, and academia present to give speeches and instructions. The exhibition of national silk, although co-organized by four organizations, was successfully completed thanks to the financial assistance of Mayor Wu of the Municipal Government and Director Wu of the Social Affairs Bureau, benefiting the silk industry. I, Lu Zhengbing, as the chairman of the Silk Industry Association, would like to express my gratitude on behalf of the industry. This year is the national goods year designated by all sectors of society. All our compatriots should work hard to promote national goods in order to seek economic prosperity. Now, let us talk about the silk industry alone. We have already realized the spirit of cooperation between the government and the people, that is, to jointly hold the National Silk Exhibition. I think that the silk industry, through this enthusiastic promotion and publicity, directly helps industry and commerce, but indirectly helps the countryside, because our country's rural areas are on the verge of bankruptcy. Therefore, Vice-President Song's establishment of wheat and cotton loans is also for the sake of helping the countryside, but the relief of our silk industry

Page 20

The relief effect is far less grand than that of wheat and cotton loans. I only hope that our compatriots will purchase durable domestic silk for all their needs. I especially hope that party and government officials and leaders from all walks of life will lead by example, so that those above will follow suit, and it will not be difficult to restore the inherent status of the past, and the rural economy will also have considerable achievements."

Chonghai Qi Five Counties Association Requests Strict Investigation and Arrest of Remaining Gang Members

丨Letter to the 4th District of the Maritime Public Security Team丨

Since the incident of the Xin Renhe ship of the Yuxing Shipping Company, after the shipowner Sun Xingsheng, the compradors Lang Xihou, Chen Baosheng, the helmsman Chen Yinglong, the crew member Feng Fusheng, and over ten others were sentenced to imprisonment by the Shanghai District Court, the defendants have now declared their dissatisfaction and have filed an appeal. The main reason for the defendants is that all four victims were gang thieves on the Shanghai-Shanhaiguan shipping lines, who openly stole from passengers and merchants. On the 18th and 30th of last month, the detective team of the 4th District of the Maritime Provincial Public Security Team arrested Jin A’er, Wu Keren, Wang Genbao, Xiao Liuzi, Shao Caiqi, Xiao Sanzi, and two unidentified individuals (arrested on the 18th) and Yu Baosheng (leader of the "Little Lion" gang), Zhang Guohua, and Wang Baohui (arrested on the 30th), a total of eleven individuals, on the Maifeng ship of the Jufeng Company. The gang leader Yu Baosheng has confessed that they are affiliated with the four victims of the Xin Renhe incident. The official letter from the Chonghai Qi Five Counties Association to Zhang Xianyi, the district chief of the 4th District of the Jiangsu Maritime Public Security Team, is transcribed below: "To the Director: According to reports from our fellow villagers Lu Renjie and Shi Xiqi, the Shanghai-Shanhaiguan shipping lines are frequently infiltrated by Yangtze River gang thieves who openly steal from passengers and merchants, and use violence. Please forward this letter to the 4th District of the Maritime Public Security to punish the arrested thieves Jin A’er and the other eight to the fullest extent of the law and send them to a vagrant vocational training center after their sentences are completed to prevent them from harming travelers." Based on this, it is found that theft has been rampant on the Shanghai-Qidong shipping line recently, and merchants and passengers are suffering. According to reports from fellow villagers traveling to and from the area, this association has already forwarded letters to your district to strictly investigate the matter. Now that the thieves Jin A’er and others have been arrested, they should be severely punished according to the law to deter violence. The original reporters' request to send them to a vagrant vocational training center after their sentences are completed is a fundamental solution, and their suggestion is very insightful. According to the report of the previous situation, we are enclosing the original documents for your reference. We hope that you will investigate and handle this matter and issue orders to your subordinates to pay close attention to the merchant ships passing through various ports on the Shanghai-Qidong line, arrest the remaining gang members, and prevent them from growing and ensure the safety of travelers. We express our sincere regards to Zhang Xianyi, the district chief of the 4th District of the Jiangsu Maritime Public Security Team."

Ou Weiguo Accused of Occupying Common Property

丨Defendant Went to Guangdong for Postponement of Further Interrogation丨

Ou Tan Huiran, the mother of Ou Weiguo, a Cantonese deputy manager of the Shanghai Bank, currently residing at No. 4 Dasheng Hutong, Lane 153, Route Haig, French Concession (also known as the wife of Ou Bin), together with fellow villagers Ye Danci (wife of dentist Ye Jingfu), Situ Chenxin, Li Zhaolanfang, Chen Ruihua, Zhao Xiaosi, and others, jointly invested 30,000 yuan (divided into 60 shares of 500 yuan each) in 1923 to establish the Women's Real Estate Company. They purchased a piece of land of ten acres behind Bazishan in Jiangwan Township, Baoshan County. After the purchase, Ou Tan Huiran, representing the Women's Real Estate Company, entrusted the British company Telifield & Co. to transfer the title deeds to British Registration No. 709. After Ou's mother, Tan Huiran, passed away from illness in October 1924, all the properties of the Women's Real Estate Company were inherited and managed by Ou Weiguo. In 1928, Ou Weiguo took out the title deeds from Telifield & Co., but he hid the deeds and refused to return them to the Women's Real Estate Company. Ye Danci, Situ Chenxin, and others repeatedly negotiated with Ou and even sent letters of demand through lawyers, but Ou ignored them. Ye Danci and others then hired lawyers to file a lawsuit in the Civil Division of the Second Special Court, accusing Ou Weiguo of occupying common property and requesting a judgment to hand over the property for joint management. After receiving the complaint, the court summoned the plaintiffs yesterday morning in the Civil Division No. 6, presided over by Judge Rao. The plaintiffs were represented by lawyer Liang Bingyao, who stated the case. The defendant was represented by lawyer Xi Shichang, who stated that the defendant had gone to Guangdong for business and requested a postponement. The court decided to set a date for further interrogation.

Linwushanren Passed Away

Mr. Bu Xiangfen, a famous scholar from Henan, styled Zhang Wu, and with the pseudonym Linwushanren, was intelligent and talented since childhood. He was known as a child prodigy. He was well-versed in all kinds of books and was skilled in classical Chinese prose, especially poetry. He entered the local school in his childhood, and in his twenties, he was recommended for the provincial examination. Later, he served in Yuan Shikai's staff as a secretary in the presidential palace for several years. After Yuan Shikai passed away, Mr. Bu came to Shanghai to live in seclusion, enjoying poetry and prose, and not seeking fame. He was fond of opera and was acquainted with people in the opera world. In recent years, he had taken in as many as two hundred actresses, enjoying the joy of being surrounded by beautiful women. Since the beginning of this summer, he suddenly suffered from a firewood-gathering disease [a metaphor for hardship]. Recently, his illness suddenly worsened, and medicine was ineffective. He passed away on the first day of this month. Another literary elder has passed away, and those who heard the news all mourned his loss. His remains are temporarily placed in the Chinese Funeral Home, and the date of the funeral will be determined after his family arrives from Henan. Xu Qianlin, Yi Junzhai, Chen Anbo, Shan Zhongfan, Feng Shuluan, Luo Tieshen, Zheng Zibao, and other gentlemen are responsible for handling the funeral affairs.

Court Summer Vacation Ends

Office Hours Return to Normal

Shen Jiayi, President of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, and Wang Zhennan, Chief Prosecutor, announced that with the end of the summer vacation, office hours should return to normal. Starting yesterday, except for Sundays and holidays, work will begin at 8:00 AM and end at 12:00 PM, and resume from 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM. In addition to ordering the affiliated First Special District Local Court and prisons to follow this schedule, they will also jointly issue a notice to inform the litigants.

Vehicles Causing Accidents Should Be Reported Immediately

The "Shanghai Evening Post" reports that personnel from the Public Concession Police Department's Traffic Division urge all drivers in Shanghai to pay attention: if involved in a traffic accident, they must immediately report to the nearby police or the Traffic Division. Even if they witness a traffic accident and are not directly involved, they should still stop and report to the police. This is their responsibility to the public. According to the traffic regulations, any vehicle directly involved in an accident must stop to assist the victims and report to the police. Violators will be punished. Recently, there have been cases where drivers have not stopped to report the accident and have been found out later, resulting in the car owners being charged and punished. Drivers are urged to pay attention to this.

Xiang Xiasheng Died From Serious Injuries

Xiang Xiasheng from Ningbo, on the evening of August 23rd at 9:00 PM, together with the fugitives A’e, Chen Xi, Zhang Quan, Xiao Biao, and others, shot and wounded his fellow villager Yan Azhang (also known as Li Azhang) in the back in a remote area of Guiyang Road, and then pushed him into a small creek, hoping to murder him. After the incident, Chen Ruhai, a Chinese detective of the Yangshupu Police Station, arrested Xiang and handed him over to Judge Wu Zehan for further interrogation. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer for the police station, stated the case, saying that the victim, Li Azhang, died in Shengxin Hospital at 10:00 AM on November 26th due to his injuries. The cause of death was that the bullet entered his back from his waist. Although the doctor removed the bullet through surgery, he could not defecate, leading to his death. It has been investigated that when these people committed the crime, they first lured Li to a dark and empty place, and then Xiao Biao and the other three surrounded Li on all sides, preventing him from escaping. A’e fired a shot, but the gun only had one bullet left. Otherwise, they would have continued to fire, fearing that he would not die from only one shot. They also took off his pants and pushed him into the creek to cover up their tracks. Their methods were cruel and their intentions were malicious. It was not to reclaim the stolen pistol. It was suspected that the victim had informed the police about Chen Xi's previous kidnapping case, resulting in resentment. At that time, they forcibly borrowed 30 yuan from the victim and, when they were refused, they gathered a gang to shoot him. The pistol did not belong to the deceased. Li Wangshi, the mother of the deceased, complained that Li Azhang was her son. After he was injured, she went to the hospital to visit him. He claimed that he was shot because he refused to lend money. When questioned, the defendant denied gathering a gang to shoot and assassinate him. After Judge Wu verified the confession, he ordered him to be remanded in custody and set a date for sentencing.

Inspection Reports of Two Banks

The Central Bank's 171st Issuance Reserve Inspection Report states: "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this Council is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds of the Bank's issuance of convertible notes. Today, August 31, 1933, we conducted the 171st inspection at the Bank's Issuance Bureau, and the results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued by the bank is 54,623,994 yuan, including 49,861,510 yuan in silver dollar notes and 4,762,484 yuan in fractional currency notes. The total amount of convertible note reserves is 54,623,994 yuan, including 44,729,994 yuan in cash reserves, which is deposited in the Bank's Issuance Vault (40,359,236 yuan), branches in various cities (2,581,144 yuan), and with fellow banks (1,789,614 yuan). The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 9,894,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued is 417,269.4 yuan, and the total amount of customs gold convertible note reserves is 417,269.4 yuan. This reserve includes 7,004.69 taels of standard gold, valued at 5957, equivalent to 417,269.4 yuan in customs gold. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's convertible note regulations, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guarantee reserve should be 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby issued." August 31, 1933, Li Fusun, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji. The inspection report of the issuance reserve of the China General Chamber of Commerce Bank states: "The issuance of convertible notes and reserves of the China General Chamber of Commerce Bank for August 1933 has now been inspected by supervisors Yu Zuoting, Fu Qilin, He Shaoyin, and Xie Jishan, together with accountant Xu Yongzuo, on September 1. The results of the inspection are listed below: The amount of convertible notes issued is 11,100,280 yuan, and the total amount of reserves is 11,100,280 yuan, including 7,313,900 yuan in cash reserves (more than 60%) and 3,786,900 yuan in guarantee reserves (less than 40%). The findings are consistent with the issuance regulations."

Letter

To the Editor:

I have read today's issue of your newspaper with the headline "Direct Train Service Between Shanghai and Pingjin Starts Tomorrow" in the local news column, and detailed information on the arrival and departure times of the trains, "The northbound train departs from Shanghai at [blank] o'clock," and "The southbound train arrives in Shanghai at 0:25 AM." After investigation, the direct train service between Shanghai and Pingjin is temporarily not direct. The northbound train on the Jinpu Line departs from Shanghai North Station at 12:00 AM, and the southbound train arrives in Shanghai at 11:55 PM. The information published in your newspaper is incorrect and presumably based on inaccurate information. Therefore, I would like to request that your newspaper make corrections immediately to avoid misunderstanding among passengers. This letter is addressed to the chief editor of the Shen Bao. Carried by the Shanghai-Nanjing-Ningbo Railway Bureau, August 31.

Acknowledgement: Thank you for the gift of the 17th issue of the 30th volume of the Eastern Miscellany from the Commercial Press.

He is expected to arrive within two or three weeks after the start of school. His exhibits and the items he exchanged with people from those countries have already been shipped in advance.

Local

From August, the Municipal Education Bureau will temporarily suspend the subsidies for private schools.

If schools need to request subsidies,

They should fill out the forms and submit them to the bureau for review within the deadline.

A notice from the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau states: After investigation by this Bureau, private primary and secondary schools in this city that are well-managed and approved for registration, and require subsidies, have been able to submit requests to this Bureau for transfer to the Municipal Government for appropriate subsidies. As the new fiscal year begins in August, these subsidies should be temporarily suspended, and a new request should be submitted according to regulations. If schools need to apply for these subsidies, they should come to the Bureau to collect the forms from September 11th to 16th, and submit the detailed forms to this Bureau for approval by September 25th. However, private primary and secondary schools within the First Special District may apply to this Bureau for permission to receive subsidies from the Public Works Department. Due to limited funds, this Bureau's direct subsidies to such schools will be temporarily suspended. This announcement is hereby made.

Shen Bao Series: On War Published

"On War" written by the famous Japanese scholar Aramaki Kanemura, is a collection of important texts on the issue of war published in major magazines from 1922 to 1932. The author, from the perspective of the masses, with a serious attitude, in-depth observation, details the theory and reality of various war theories. The book is divided into eight chapters, totaling more than 60,000 words. Anyone who wants to understand the nature and meaning of modern imperialist wars, the prediction of the Second World War, the Pacific and Manchurian problems, and the wars between capitalist and socialist countries, must read this book. It is now translated by Mr. Shen Zijiu, and the translation is fluent and the writing is lively. The actual price is only 35 cents. This newspaper has a special distribution. During this autumn school season, there is a special price for one month. If you buy 10 or more copies, you will get a 30% discount.

Ministry of Interior Approves Guangzhao Middle School's Land Requisition for Construction of School Buildings

Announcement No. 33 of the Ministry of Interior on Land: The Shanghai Municipal Government has transferred the report from the Shanghai Guangzhao Association, stating that the Guangzhao Public School established by the association has insufficient school buildings and plans to build a large-scale and fully-equipped middle school, and should pay attention to the implementation of vocational education. Therefore, in addition to adding ordinary high schools, vocational high schools of commerce, civil engineering, machinery, and mining will be added. In addition to the various buildings required for the construction of ordinary middle schools, four large-scale factories will be added in phases for students of various vocational subjects to practice on-site. It has been surveyed and determined that an area of land near the Jiangwan Water and Electricity Road, with a total area of 200 mu, needs to be requisitioned, excluding the 18 mu already purchased, with 182 mu still needing to be requisitioned for construction. The funds for land purchase and construction have also been prepared properly. According to this, the relevant charts and other documents are enclosed for review and reply. Only this, after verification, is in accordance with the provisions of the first half of Article 2, Paragraph 7 of the Land Requisition Law, and should be approved. In addition to replying for investigation and handling, please still handle it in accordance with the law and pay a fair price. It is imperative to list the matters that should be announced in accordance with the provisions of Article 9 of the same law, so that the public will know. A special announcement is hereby made, including: 1. The person running the business: Shanghai Guangzhao Association. 2. The type of business: education and academic business. 3. The area where the business is run: Jiangwan Water and Electricity Road, Shanghai, with a total land area of 182 mu. August 18, 22nd year, September 1, 22nd year.

Restrictions on Distributing Publications at the National Games Venue

Preventing the infiltration of reactionary publications

Shanxi reports participation in men's and women's groups.

Gansu telegraphed that they had set off for Ningxia.

(Nanjing, 1st dispatch) With the opening of the National Games approaching, it is heard that various parties have reported printed special editions, etc., for publicity. The Propaganda Group of the Organizing Committee, in order to prevent reactionary publications and leaflets from taking the opportunity to infiltrate and disrupt the order of the Games, all kinds of publications and leaflets distributed or sold at the venue must be submitted to the Group for review in advance to show seriousness. In addition to reactionary publications, which will be strictly prohibited and investigated, publications and leaflets containing business advertisements will also not be distributed at the venue. Participants who continue to report to the National Games are: Shanxi to participate in women's groups and Gansu telegraphed that they have set off for Ningxia, and will come to Beijing after participating in the three-province Games.

In addition, the National Games Organizing Committee has stipulated the registration method for news reporters. Each newspaper is limited to one registered person per event, and registration will start on the first day.

Track and field competitions concluded, today's ball game competitions
