Survival After Calamity

Famous Generals from the Northeast Arrive in Shanghai Together

Fu Baolu Yu Xiwei Wang Mingshen Wu Jingyao

Shanghai's Track and Field Strength Doubled in the National Games

The former five tiger women generals (Sun Guiyun, Wu Meixian, Liu Jingzhen, Wang Yuan, Xiao Shuling) from Harbin shocked the country. On the men's side, Fu Baolu set the highest national pole vault record with 3.54 meters. In recent North China Games and Hangzhou National Games, Yu Xiwei, a middle-distance runner from Dalian, and Wang Mingshen and Wu Jingyao, short-distance and long-distance runners from Liaoning, have repeatedly shown their skills and are famous throughout the country. They are the most memorable figures in China's track and field circles. However, since the fall of the Northeast, the athletes have been in danger and under strict surveillance by pseudo-organizations. Therefore, their news has been lost for a long time. Recently, they suddenly escaped from the tiger's mouth and came to Shanghai to study together, and plan to represent Shanghai in the National Games. This is really gratifying. Here are the latest developments of each person:

Fu Baolu

Fu is the record holder for the pole vault in our country, and recently unofficially reached a height of 3.80 meters, which is amazing. He also said that in this year's National Games, it is not difficult to break through 3.60 meters. He has now arrived in Shanghai and plans to seek a part-time job to continue his studies on the one hand, and to maintain his livelihood on the other. He plans to represent Shanghai in the Nanjing National Games.

Yu Xiwei

Last year, there was a plan to send Yu and Liu Changchun to represent our country at the 10th World Games, but Yu could not escape the cage at that time, and did not get his wish. Now Yu has also arrived in Shanghai and plans to study in Shanghai. His highest record for 800 meters is 2 minutes and 2 seconds. If the field is good, he can make 2 minutes. The 1500 meters is around 4 minutes and 15 seconds, which is valuable. He also plans to represent Shanghai in the National Games.

Wang Mingshen

Wang is a famous middle-distance runner, comparable to Yu Xiwei. He currently holds the national record for 800 meters at 2 minutes 6.8 seconds, and the 1500 meters is about 4 minutes and 25 seconds. He has arrived in Shanghai and plans to represent Shanghai in the National Games, but must continue his studies.

Wu Jingyao

During the 15th North China Games in Jinan, Wu Jun first emerged in the intermediate group, winning three championships in the 100m, 100m, and 400m events. The results were quite outstanding, and he was known as the second Liu Changchun. However, times have changed, and due to environmental factors, he failed to continue to add glory to the North China Games. His recent results are 11.6 seconds for 100m and 23.8 seconds for 200m. He is a new short-distance runner. Today, he and Yu Xiwei and others arrived in Shanghai, and plan to represent Shanghai in the National Games.

National Sports Association Convened a Meeting of Representatives from Various Regions

The term of office of the directors and standing committee members of the Chinese National Sports Association has expired. According to the regulations, the National Congress of Representatives should be convened to elect the successors. The Board of Directors decided on August 3, 20th year, to convene the National Congress of Representatives in Beijing at the time of the National Games, in accordance with the National Games method, with the province and special city as the unit, to discuss the development of association affairs. Due to the impact of the situation, the National Games were postponed, and the association was also adjourned. This year's National Games are scheduled to be held in Beijing on the Double Tenth Festival. The association has also decided to convene a representative conference in Beijing during the National Games, and has sent letters to the sports bureaus of various provinces and cities and sports figures, requesting them to send one representative to attend the meeting.

Takahashi 2000 Meter Sea Swim to be Held Tomorrow

Enthusiastic Participation

The Takahashi 2000-meter sea swimming competition is scheduled to be held tomorrow. For safety, the organizers have prepared six lifeboats and one speedboat, each equipped with four lifebuoys and one rescuer. Those wishing to participate in the competition or watch can take the city ferry from the Bund on the main road in the morning and transfer to a car, making transportation very convenient. The prizes include a silver shield from the mayor for the first place winner, a silver cup from the chairman for the second place winner, and cups and shields from various bureau chiefs for subsequent places. All those who swim to the finish within fifty minutes will receive award flags and medals. The competition time is set from noon to 2 PM, as this is during the time of slack tide, making it safer and more stable. All previous participants should report to the Takahashi Hotel on time. New participants are also welcome. Today at 4 PM

At Jiaotong University, Xujiahui

American Baseball Home Run King Babe Ruth Hopes to Become a Manager

Leg Injury Hinders Running

To End Competition After This Season

(New York, August 31, Reuters) American baseball home run king Babe Ruth, known to all, intends to end his career as a baseball player and pursue a managerial position. He stated, "This season will be my last. After this, I will give up my playing position and hope to become a manager of a team." Ruth was once surpassed by his rival, Jimmy Foxx, but soon regained his title as king. Ruth is an excellent pitcher, but his outstanding hitting skills have led him to play as an outfielder. However, since injuring his leg last year, although he has shown remarkable performances, his running has been hindered, leading him to seek another path and announce his intention to become a manager.

A Dual-Purpose Machine for Learning Morse Code and Testing Vacuum Tubes

— Yi Zhi

Friends who enjoy listening to or working with radio technology, do you aspire to become a radio operator or a radio technician? Then you should quickly practice sending and receiving Morse code. Code substitutes for language and can be transmitted through radio to send messages. Code also has unique advantages: the transmitter for sending code is simpler in construction than a voice transmitter, and the transmission distance is several times greater than that of a voice transmitter. Because of its special and impressive efficiency, all countries in the world use it to transmit messages. Learning to send and receive code is not difficult. As long as you memorize the code and practice sending and receiving for about two to three months, you will surely succeed. Receiving foreign telegrams is as easy as listening to the radio, and sending code is also very convenient. Whether you are hundreds or thousands of miles apart, it is as if you are together, speaking face-to-face. What an interesting experience!

There are usually two types of machines for learning to send and receive code: one uses a buzzer and the other uses an audio frequency oscillator. The sound of the former is weaker and the tone is inferior to the latter, but it also has its advantages: it is cheaper and easier to use. The latter, using an audio frequency oscillator, requires a vacuum tube and an audio frequency transformer to be properly matched to create oscillation. In the oscillation circuit, a key is connected in series. Pressing and releasing the key emits a buzzing sound, just like a telegram, for practicing sending and receiving.

This code learning device is also a dual-purpose machine for testing vacuum tubes. It is powered by AC electricity, which makes it small, consumes little power, and is convenient to use. This machine is very easy to assemble. Most of the components required are probably already available to radio enthusiasts, so it is very economical. The required materials are listed below:

One 227 vacuum tube

One 201A vacuum tube

One power transformer

One audio frequency transformer

One key

Two 2MFD filter capacitors

One 30H choke coil

One headset or speaker

One four-pin tube socket

One five-pin tube socket

One 2.5V small light bulb

Plugs, screws, and wiring

Once all the components are ready, you can start assembling. The wiring diagram is shown in Figure 1. V1 is a 227 tube, V2 is a 201A tube (I71, 280, etc. tubes can also be used), T is the power transformer, T1 is the audio frequency transformer, K is the key, C1C2 are filter capacitors, L is the choke coil (a burnt audio frequency transformer can be used with its secondary coil to replace it), P is the headset, L.S. is the speaker, R is a variable resistor, and B is a small light bulb.

After connecting all the wires according to Figure 1, plug the plug into a 220-volt or 110-volt power line. Press and release the key and gradually reduce the resistance until you hear a sound similar to a telegram in the headset or speaker. If there is no sound in the headset or speaker, there must be a wiring error. Unplug the plug from the power line, carefully check the circuit for errors, and then try reversing the two wires of the audio frequency transformer. If there is still no sound, the 227 tube may be too old and has lost its efficiency, so it cannot oscillate. Try replacing it with a new one.

Based on the above principle, testing whether a vacuum tube oscillates can determine its efficiency. The testing method is the same as above. Insert a new vacuum tube, reduce the variable resistance until you hear a sound in the headset or speaker. Remove the new vacuum tube and insert the vacuum tube to be tested. Test it in the same way to see if it can also oscillate. Increase or decrease the resistance to determine its efficiency. If you want to determine the efficiency accurately, the resistor should be wire-wound and labeled with numbers like 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, etc. for easy recording, as shown in Figure 2. This method can also be used to test tetrodes or pentodes. Just slightly adjust the wiring on the V1 vacuum tube socket or change the key to open and close it. The wiring diagrams are shown in Figures 3 and 4, one for testing tetrodes and one for testing pentodes.

Essential Knowledge for Long-Distance Radio Reception

— Li Yuanqing

In America, a seventeen-year-old boy can receive broadcasts from all over the world (41 countries, 694 stations) with a very ordinary two-tube radio. However, some people use fifteen-tube radios and cannot cross the Atlantic. Someone in Nanjing can hear Japanese broadcasts with a crystal radio, but someone else in the same location uses an eight-tube superheterodyne radio and cannot receive Shanghai broadcasts. Therefore, the distance a radio can receive is not entirely dependent on the quality of the radio itself. It is also closely related to other factors. The following points are very important.

1. Raise and lengthen the antenna. The lead-in wire should preferably be connected directly to the antenna (see "Improved Single-Wire Antenna" in Issue 5 of this publication). Otherwise, it must be soldered. The ground wire should be as deep as possible. (Note: The higher the antenna, the better, but it should not be too long. Too long an antenna will have poor selectivity and more noise. It is best to keep it between 100 and 150 feet.)

2. Vacuum tubes must be replaced after one year or 1,000 hours of use. Whether a vacuum tube is damaged internally is not determined by whether it lights up or not. Do not buy cheap, no-name vacuum tubes.

3. Even vacuum tubes of the same brand and manufacturer will not have exactly the same characteristics. Some are suitable for detection, while others are suitable for amplification. When using them, they should be rotated in the radio to achieve the best performance.

4. The voltage of each electrode of each vacuum tube must be according to the specified values. Too high or too low is not appropriate.

5. The grid leak of the detector tube is best to be variable. Otherwise, several resistors with different values must be prepared. When receiving distant broadcasts, a 2 megohm grid leak is often too small and should be replaced with a 3.5 megohm grid leak.

6. Adding a regeneration coil to the radio will greatly improve its sensitivity. Adding one or two stages of high-frequency amplification will have an even more unexpected effect.

7. Adding a 1/2 mfd fixed capacitor between the earphone end and B+ and B- can increase the sensitivity of the radio and improve the sound quality.

8. The sensitivity of the earphone or speaker is also very important. Many poorly made speakers or earphones can only receive local or loud broadcasts. Weak signals cannot make them produce sound.

9. The distance a radio can receive is shorter during the day than at night, worse in summer than in winter, and shorter in the tropics than in cold regions, shorter in cities than in the countryside.

10. Radio waves from distant locations travel a long distance and are prone to fading (new radios with automatic volume control can avoid this). Therefore, receiving distant broadcasts requires patience. At the same time, considerable training is required in tuning.

Simple Antennas

— Zhu Ziyuan

I have tried both of the following simple antennas, and the effect is no different from that of an outdoor antenna. I am writing about them here so that you can try them out.

A. Using a telephone line as an antenna is extremely simple. Simply connect the telephone wire entering the house to the antenna terminal of the radio with a piece of rubber wire. However, it is important to connect a 0.001 to 0.005 microfarad fixed capacitor in series here. Otherwise, the telephone will not work, as shown in Figure 1.

B. Using a power line as an antenna. There are three ways to connect it, as shown in Figures 2A, B, and C.

A is to use only one of the power lines. The best one to use must be determined by experimentation.

B is to use both wires as an antenna.

C is to not use a ground wire.

I think method A is the best of these three methods, and method C is the worst. In method C, the capacitor must be able to withstand high voltage, and the capacitance is from 0.002 to 2 microfarads.

When I tested the above two simple antennas with a regenerative single-tube radio in Songjiang, there was no difference from the outdoor antenna. At night, I could also listen to K2RM's light and clear Western music. If a comrade testing a transmitter wants to listen to broadcasts from other places at the same time, then they can install one less outdoor antenna.

If you encounter a time when tuning is not sensitive, you can add an extra coil and a variable capacitor (please refer to Q.S.P. Magazine, Volume 2, Issue 1). I will not discuss it in detail here.

Shortwave Transmitter Tuning Method and Steps (Continued)

— Luo Jingyu

(D) Plate-Grid Resonance: This type of circuit also uses capacitive coupling; however, it relies on the capacitance (C3 in the figure) between the plate and grid of the vacuum tube itself to feed the plate current back to the grid and cause oscillation.

Because the capacitance of the vacuum tube itself is very small and the feedback energy is not high, it is suitable for general shortwave transmitters. Also, because its capacitance is fixed inside the vacuum tube and cannot be adjusted at will to determine the ratio of excitation between the plate and grid, C2 is specially placed in the grid circuit in Figure 3 for control. When we perform tuning, first set C1 to half (that is, at the 50-degree mark on the dial), then rotate C2 from zero degrees gradually increasing, while the reading on the plate milliammeter AIP also gradually increases. When C2 is rotated to a certain degree, the plate current reading suddenly drops from its maximum to zero. If C2 is further rotated, the plate current gradually increases again, and when it reaches a certain degree, it again drops from its maximum to zero. The point where the plate current drops is the best standard point for the oscillation situation we want to obtain. However, in practical applications, the grid C2 is usually slightly increased in degrees to keep the plate current 10% higher than the minimum to ensure the stability of the wavelength. Also, after changing the grid capacitance C2, the wave-determining C2 must also be adjusted accordingly, otherwise the wavelength will not match the original one.

As for the other circuits, because they are generally derived from these three main circuits, although some places are different, the main principles can be inferred from this. The tuning procedure is only slightly different in terms of complexity. Also, during the tuning process, it is advisable to use a wavemeter to check at any time, otherwise it will be a waste of effort if you succeed but do not achieve the goal. (To be continued)

A Collection of Vacuum Tubes (Continued)

— Ke Ming

Tetrodes have the disadvantage of excessive regeneration due to the grid-screen capacitance, but it can be reduced or eliminated by several methods. One method is to use complex circuitry and coordination to generate a reaction that balances the coupling between the grid and the screen. A second and better method is to minimize the grid-screen capacitance within the tube itself. This can be accomplished by inserting a fourth electrode called a screen grid inside the tube. The screen grid is placed between the plate and the grid, thus forming a tetrode. Using this type of tube eliminates the need for complex circuits and balancing difficulties. Since the screen voltage can effectively control the flow of electrons, small changes in the plate voltage will not significantly affect the plate current. This is important for stability. The structure of the screen grid does not substantially block the electron flow, but it provides an electrostatic shield between the plate and the grid. The voltage of the screen grid is a positive voltage lower than the plate voltage and is connected to the cathode via a capacitor branch. This bypass capacitor introduces the screen grid current or high-frequency current to the ground and minimizes the grid-screen capacitance. Generally, the grid-screen capacitance of an average triode is 8.0 MMF, while in a screen grid tube, it can be reduced to 0.01 MMF or even less. As a result of the reduction, the stable amplification of a screen grid tube can exceed that of a triode many times over. Representative tubes of this type are 24丨A, '32, and '35.

Pentodes: In various radio tubes, when electrons strike the plate at considerable speed, some electrons can be ejected from the plate. In diodes or triodes, this ejection of electrons does not pose a problem because there is no other positive electrode in the tube besides the plate itself to attract them; they are ultimately collected back by the plate. The electrons emitted from the plate after being struck by electrons from the cathode are called secondary emission. The term "secondary" distinguishes them from the electrons originally emitted by the cathode. In screen grid tubes, the screen grid also has a positive voltage close to the plate voltage, which attracts the secondary electrons, especially when the plate voltage drops below the screen voltage. This results in a reduction of the plate current and limits the rise and fall of the tetrode's plate voltage.

To eliminate the limitation of plate current, a fifth electrode called a suppressor grid is added between the screen and the plate, thus creating a pentode. The suppressor grid is usually connected to the cathode. Because it is at a negative potential relative to the plate, it prevents the ejection of secondary electrons and redirects them back to the plate, where they do not cause any problems. Currently, the design of the suppressor grid in pentodes can be divided into two functions. In power output pentodes, the suppressor grid can maximize the power output and gain of the pentode because the plate voltage can have extremely large swings. Representative tubes of this type are '33, '38, and '47. In high-frequency amplification pentodes, the suppressor grid can achieve high voltage amplification at normal plate voltages. In fact, the plate voltage can be as low as or even lower than the screen voltage without significantly losing the possible amount of gain. These tubes can be represented by '34 and '39. The design of the tube, with the suppressor grid also connected to the outside of the base, can yield additional benefits and applications. Because of this, it is possible to change the voltage applied to the suppressor grid to achieve special control purposes. Standard tubes of this type are 57 and 58. (End)

How to Repair Damaged Headphones

— RF

Headphones are easily damaged if not used carefully, resulting in weak sound or complete silence. The following describes the repair methods for those who wish to repair them themselves.

(1) Demagnetization: Headphones that have lost their magnetism produce faint sound. The remedy is to remagnetize them. The method is to take out the permanent magnet inside and wind it with 100 to 200 turns of No. 18 silk-covered wire, then pass a current from a 6-volt storage battery for about one second. Then, reinstall it as it was, and the sound should be as loud as usual. (The wiring and connection of electricity should be as shown in the figure. The N pole in the figure is the pole that attracts the south-pointing needle of a compass. If there is no storage battery, dry batteries or the current used to replace the A battery that can supply a large current can also be used.)

(2) Diaphragm Damage: Headphones with a damaged diaphragm produce rough sound. You need to replace it with a new diaphragm to improve the sound. You can replace it with a soft iron sheet of the same thickness and size. (If you cannot find a soft iron sheet for the time being, you can cut a thin iron sheet from a 50-cigarette tin or a high-quality biscuit tin to replace it.)

(3) Broken Wire: Headphones with a broken wire produce no sound after being energized or may have occasional popping sounds. You can first use a multimeter to check where the break is. If the broken wire is silk-covered soft wire, you can replace the broken wire with the cord wire used for electric lamps. If the broken wire is the fine enamel wire inside the earphone, you can remove all the broken wire and replace it with No. 44 enamel wire in the original pattern.

Common Sense

— Huang Jiancun

(14) Detector Circuit

(1) Meaning of Detection: When an external radio wave is absorbed by the antenna, a radio-frequency current will inevitably be generated in the antenna. To enable the headphones to fully perform their sound-receiving function, it is necessary to first decompose the radio-frequency current generated in the antenna and extract the audio-frequency current contained therein. The device that performs this function is called a detector.

(2) Detector: In the detector circuit, the most important component is the detector, whose function is detection. There are many types of detectors. Branly invented a type of Coherer detector in 1892, which consists of a metal tube filled with metal electrodes and metal powder (a mixture of nickel and silver powder) between the metal electrodes. When a radio wave arrives, the incomplete contact between the metal particles immediately becomes complete contact. This effect is used for detection. Marconi used it for radio communication at the time. It was the ancestor of detectors, but this type of detector is no longer used. Currently, the most commonly used types are crystal detectors and vacuum tube detectors. Radios that use crystals for detection are called crystal radios, while those that use vacuum tubes for detection are called vacuum tube radios.

(3) Crystal Detector: A crystal that performs detection is called a crystal detector. The operation of the crystal detector is explained in the diagram above. As shown in the diagram, because a radio-frequency current passes through the antenna, a high-frequency voltage is generated at both ends of the coil, so the current also flows into the crystal. However, the current flowing into the crystal only flows in one direction. This is because the crystal detector has a unidirectional characteristic. The so-called unidirectional characteristic means that the flow of current is limited to one direction, and it cannot flow in the other direction. Thus, only a half-wave current flows into the headphones, so the diaphragm of the headphones must vibrate with the strength of the current and ultimately move with the audio current contained in the external radio wave.

Spring and Autumn

River Management Discourse

— Qing Qu

The Yellow River in Shandong Province had its water level suddenly drop due to breaches in the provinces of Hebei and Henan, and it could be considered out of danger. Unexpectedly, the river suddenly breached in eighteen locations at Shitou Village, with the water all returning to the main river. This caused a rapid rise in the torrent in the middle reaches, even exceeding the highest water level, a new record for the month. According to River Bureau Director Zhang Lianjia, the water in the Shouzhang and Fanxian areas crossed the northern bank's Golden Dike, reaching eighteen inches. Although rescue efforts are underway, the danger has not yet passed. How terrifying is this "flood disaster"?

I think that when the divine Yu managed the waters in ancient times, he first dredged the Dragon Gate, then guided the Jishi, and then breached the Ru and Han, draining the Huai and Si. Looking at the sequence of his work, it was simply about following the nature of the water, allowing the rolling torrent to flow into the sea! And the overwhelming floods in ancient China were thus calmed, allowing our people to live in peace, without having to live together with the aquatic creatures. This is all thanks to the great achievements of King Yu. Now, the officials managing the river, I dare to boldly say, are "imitating Bai Gui's old tricks," hastily building several dikes and adding a few embankments when faced with imminent danger, considering it to be the limit of human effort. Therefore, when the Yellow River breaches and floods in the autumn, we hear the news every year. Alas! This is a "man-made disaster," not attributable to the natural world. Yet, people knit their brows in anger, calling it a "natural disaster." I fear that if Heaven knew, it would truly be unbearable!

Why do I say this? Try to look through the river management history that we can see. Not to mention the distant past, let's talk about the recent past. The so-called "river works" item, I don't know how much money is spent during the alarm period. And what is the result later? Alas! It is a major leak in the nation's finances. And from the perspective of officialdom, it has become a huge source of incalculable profits. This is not an exaggeration on my part. In fact, the writings of the predecessors clearly show this, leaving no room for denial. Later, although there are defense projects and relief preparation plans, they can all be said to be last-minute efforts. Considering them to be "treating the symptoms" is not enough. Where does the method of "treating the root cause" begin?

The reason lies in the first step of "not understanding the source." Therefore, in the transition between summer and autumn, there is often accumulated rain and lurking floods, with the force of a thousand miles in one go. Moreover, there are countless places where dikes and embankments collapse. People don't pay attention to it on weekdays, and wait until the water flows freely, inundating countless fields and crops, and then urgently report the disaster. You! Think, is it still in time? The second step, if you want to avoid river disasters, lies in "filling and building" and "excavating." Then, you need to purchase the latest machines to achieve even the slightest effect. Sending a few technicians will not have much power to show to the affected people. Third, even if you have "capable officials," you still need extraordinary amounts of money to achieve world-shaking achievements. May I ask, can the current government, with its depleted national currency, afford to spend so much at once, while the benefits can last for generations? Therefore, "river disasters" are not only a major problem for our country at present, but I believe they will also be a major problem in the future. It is necessary to plan a permanent solution to the problem.

Autumn Colors

— Qian Taisheng

Autumn has arrived, hasn't it? The thermometer has dropped from ninety-eight degrees to seventy-three.

In fruit stores, there are more and more bunches of purple-black rose grapes, marked at thirty-five copper coins apiece. Not a penny less. They're the new season's goods, why wouldn't they be holding "premium prices"?

Red flesh, black seeds, green-skinned watermelons, shouting loudly in the middle of the street:

"Three copper coins a slice! Fresh, sweet, cool watermelon!"

Autumn has arrived, but watermelons should still be eaten sparingly! That shouting assistant, he doesn't even have the strength to squeeze a fist! Look! Look at the way he's shouting!

Ginkgo nuts are on the market! A broken iron wok, a big pile of broken ceramic pieces, using a small spatula, shoveling inside the broken iron wok. Listen:

"Clang, clang, singing, clang, clang, singing, dismantling lalala......"

A small yellow clay stove, a small iron wire basket with small holes, grabbing a handful of wet ginkgo nuts, turning around, the spatula in his hand shoveling the ceramic pieces. Listen to the assistant sing:

"Fragrant is fragrant, glutinous is glutinous, three copper coins for one, one grain blooms, two grains grow big (pronounced tuo)......"

In the broken wok, ceramic pieces grabbing ceramic pieces, an iron spatula hitting the iron wok, the sound is:

"Dismantling lalala, clang, clang, singing, dismantling lalala......" Poetic rhythm, dramatic air, isn't the melody simple and beautiful? It's truly street mime, the sounds of autumn in the city!

Big store signs, big red paper flying characters, Yan style or Zhao style? Writing:

"New Autumn Mooncakes on the Market"

Guangdong mooncakes, local mooncakes, it's only the beginning of the seventh lunar month. By the Mid-Autumn Festival, when "the moon is especially bright," I'm afraid the tips of people's tongues will be tired of eating them. Truly city dwellers who are rushing to the early market!

Tianjin "Liangxiang" chestnuts, in the sweet, greasy calling of fresh lotus root, Tianjin apples, deep brown-yellow chestnuts, in that big iron wok, exuding a charming fragrance, that rich starch and red sugar fragrance that hooks the hungry urban crowd, is truly enough to make people endure!

Supporting Role

— Lin Ying

It was an early autumn evening.

At Mr. Lin's wedding banquet, Miss Nen, the bridesmaid, always showed boredom and depression.

"Alas! Today is truly extremely meaningless, a whole day!" she said in a low voice.

"It's very meaningful!"

I said, not expecting her mood.

"Always playing the supporting role! Ah."

"Do you want to play the leading role? Girl!" A golden, strong wine was shimmering in front of her.

"Oh! Who cares!"

In her rosy cheeks, the strong wine moistened her red lips.

No Matter How You Are......Always......

— Ren

No matter how lively you are, after death, you will never be alive again. You must listen to the barber's manipulation with all your attention. No matter how shy you are, when you take a bath in a public bathhouse, there is no way to think about it.

No matter how impatient you are, you can't do anything if you meet a slow doctor.

No matter how lazy you are, you always have to do it, pulling your stool and draining your urine. No matter how slow you are, when it's time to get on the train? You always have to run a few steps in a hurry.

Beautiful Dusk

— Zhang Bai'ou

Unwilling to let down this beautiful dusk, I ran out of the study I had been living in for a day, and expressed boundless reveries to the setting sun that was about to sink below the horizon. It was not until its tip, like the tongue of a wheel-like flame, became thin red clouds that my sight was drawn back from the sky to a rural village surrounded by trees and water. On the roofs and treetops of that rural village, layers of dark-green illusory clouds were piled up, constantly changing into images of everything on earth. There were craggy mountain peaks, terraced pavilions, and undulating fierce beasts, which were vividly described in Gu Kaizhi's poem: "Summer clouds have many strange peaks." When experiencing it personally, I feel that the poet's inspiration is particularly richer than that of ordinary people, giving us the joy of depicting and reflecting. It is a pity that I do not have a single drop of poetic juice in my chest. Otherwise, facing the beautiful scenery in front of me, I could put my hands behind my back and chant for a while.

The twilight gradually covered up, but the crescent moon, less than half-full, hanging on the top of the evergreen tree gradually emitted its clear light. No matter how the god of night used its huge iron wings to cover up the darkness, it could not cover up the bright eyes of sister moon. Sprinkled on the branches, roofs, fields, rivers, mountains, streams, etc. is its universally loving silver light. She stands among the stars, like a benevolent empress, accepting the worship of all things covered by her.

I stood there silently, just standing there, the rushing thoughts could not escape beyond this free world. The fields where new rice has ripened seem to be a realm of pearls in the moonlight, and it also makes people associate it with coral reefs on the seabed. The red flowers of the kapok tree are like beacons for night travelers. The waterfall of the nearby mountain in the shadows is particularly spectacular in the moonlight. The fishing boats parked under the big trees on the river bank are radiating one or two points of light from their awnings, which echoes the shimmering fireflies on the water's edge. Autumn insects have sounded their first movement, and everything, everything is smiling humorously in the moonlight.

A faint, clear feeling grew up from my heart. The brain nerves that had been muddied by the sultry air and the children's noise during the day were completely dispersed and completely clear at this time. Such a beautiful dusk, I really don't want to run back into the low, humid, and mosquito-filled room.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 14: Difficult Marriage, Lingering Worries about the Future, Small Gathering with Friends, Bashful Remembrance of the Past

He lowered his head and walked straight forward when he suddenly heard someone shouting in front of him: Here he comes, here he comes! Isn't this exactly him coming? Zhao Ziqiang looked up and saw that it was Tian Qing and Huang Manying standing and laughing at the door of his house. Zhao Ziqiang smiled and said: How did you two meet here? Tian Qing smiled and said: Came to drink your wedding wine. Zhao Ziqiang smiled and said: Stop being naughty, it is not appropriate to joke here. As he spoke, he raised his foot to walk inside the house. Tian Qing stretched out both hands, blocking the door, and smiled: Don't go in, I have a few words to say to you. Let's go to the milk tea shop, eat a bowl of yuanxiao, okay? Zhao Ziqiang said: Wait for me, I have met... Tian Qing grabbed one of Zhao Ziqiang's arms and dragged him away without allowing him to explain. Before leaving, he threw a wink at Huang Manying, and she did not follow. Zhao Ziqiang walked along the road, complaining: You are really unreasonable. I haven't been home for many days and am eager to say a few words to my father, but you don't care and drag me away. Tian Qing smiled and said: I have already told the old man there, he said it doesn't matter, but don't make too much noise with the jokes. Zhao Ziqiang said: What? Do you want to joke with me? Tian Qing smiled and said: It's nothing, just talking. As he spoke, he had already arrived at the entrance of the milk tea shop. Zhao Ziqiang couldn't not go in, so he had to follow him in. When they got inside, the waiter asked them to sit in the loose seats in the general area. Tian Qing said: We have four people, so we have to occupy a private room. The waiter smiled and said: Okay! Please come to the private room. As he spoke, he rolled up the curtain, letting the two of them in. Zhao Ziqiang said: Where are there four people? Tian Qing smiled and said: There are also our lovers. Zhao Ziqiang said: Of course, Miss Huang is coming, who else? Tian Qing smiled and said: There is... No need to ask, they will come in a while. Zhao Ziqiang really couldn't think of what his plans were. He had no choice but to order cocoa from the waiter and drink it slowly. (176)

Small Recipe

Cooking and Nutrition of Tofu

— Bing Yu

Tofu is my favorite food in my entire life. Whether the cooking method is simple or complex, it always has a special flavor. A simple way to eat it is to take a piece of soft tofu, add a few drops of sesame oil, a pinch of fine salt, mix well, and it becomes very delicious. In addition, you can mix it with Toona sinensis and sesame paste, or add some red fermented bean curd marinade, or use pickled vegetable marinade to cook it. These are all very simple and economical. If you cook it in a complex way, like the dozens of methods in Mr. Yuan Zicai's "Suiyuan Shidan," those methods are not suitable for ordinary families because they require a lot of ingredients and procedures, completely losing the original meaning of eating tofu. Now, I will talk about the economical cooking methods of tofu and its nutritional benefits:

1. Nutritional Benefits of Tofu: According to scholars' research and analysis, the nutritional components of tofu are: moisture 88.7%, protein 6.5%, fat 0.3%, carbohydrate 3.7%, calcium 0.5%, iron 0.02%, phosphorus 0.23%, salt 0.25%, calories 45. Vitamin B is the most abundant, and vitamins A and D are also present. Therefore, people who have beriberi or eye diseases should eat more tofu. If people with diabetes eat tofu every day, they can be cured naturally. Nowadays, well-known nutritionists all recognize tofu as an indispensable food. Other benefits include that eating tofu can detoxify alcohol, prevent poisoning from bacteria, animal meat, and fish meat. When stung by bees, applying tofu can neutralize the toxins and dissipate them outwards. If you use tofu to wash the fur of domestic animals such as dogs and cats, it can completely remove dirt and scars from the skin, and the fur color will also be very shiny. Also, drying tofu in the sun can be used as a substitute for facial cleansing powder. In the past, the beauty method of Fujianese women was to wipe their faces with tofu, so their complexion was very delicate. As for the method of selecting tofu, it is very simple. The best quality tofu should be white and tender, soft and slippery to the touch, and melt in the mouth. Hard and old tofu will have a bitter taste and is not easily

digested. However, old tofu and soft tofu each have different effects depending on the cooking method.

2. Economical Cooking Methods of Tofu: There are many ways to cook tofu. Now, what I am going to talk about is very economical and delicious. Moreover, eating it with this cooking method is more beneficial than eating delicacies. If you don't believe it, please try eating it for a month, and you will feel that your appetite is increased and all diseases are eliminated. (1) Stir-frying method: There are many ways to stir-fry, but often people do not get the method right, which not only makes it unpalatable but also loses the nutrients. Therefore, when stir-frying, one should pay full attention. The most beneficial stir-fried tofu dish is spinach stir-fried tofu. Spinach is rich in vitamins A and B. The stir-frying method is: first cut the tofu into small pieces, use a ladle of oil. When the oil is hot and smoking, put the tofu in and fry both sides until golden brown. Sprinkle a pinch of salt, then add a bowl of clear water, cover the pot, and let it boil. Then add the chopped spinach, boil again, add a little soy sauce, uncover the pot, and slowly remove from the pot. Generally, people with intestinal problems are very suitable to eat it. Another is garlic stir-fried tofu. Garlic has the effects of preventing diseases, disinfecting, strengthening the stomach, and removing toxins in medicine. People in northern China like to eat it the most, so their bodies are very strong. This cooking method is also very simple. First cut the tofu into small pieces, let it dry, and dry-fry it with a little oil for three minutes and set aside. Then put the sliced garlic into the pot and stir-fry until cooked, then mix in the stir-fried tofu, and sprinkle a little salt and soy sauce at the same time, a ladle of cooking wine, and dozens of dried shrimps (dried shrimps must be boiled in boiling water for one hour). Stir-fry for five minutes and remove from the pot. Other methods of stir-frying tofu with Chinese cabbage or rapeseed can still be cooked according to the spinach method. (2) Stewing method: The most important thing to pay attention to in the stewing method is that the stewing time should be long and the cooking time should be short. The tofu to be stewed should be old, and the tofu to be cooked should be soft. Old tofu will not open up if it is stewed for a short time (that is, the tofu becomes honeycomb-like after being stewed over low heat). Soft tofu will crumble into pieces if it is cooked for too long. The above cooking methods are simple, economical, and rich in nutrients, because turnips contain a lot of vitamins A and E and iron, and mushrooms contain vitamin D. People who are vegetarian usually rely on the nutritional power of tofu and green vegetables.
